                  <hi rend="ital">Conformation, or proportion,</hi> of a man or beast; <hi rend="ital">lineament</hi> of the face: <hi rend="ital">i. q.</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">قَدٌّ</foreign>, of a man: (K:) and the <hi rend="ital">stature;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">justness, or beauty, of the stature;</hi> of a man; syn. <foreign lang="ar">قَامَةٌ</foreign>: (K:) and the <hi rend="ital">cut, shape, fashion,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">form,</hi> of anything: see an ex. voce <foreign lang="ar">زَبَنٌ</foreign>; and also voce <foreign lang="ar">قَدٌّ</foreign>, where it is shown that, being an attribute of a thing as well as of a person, it does not always mean <hi rend="ital">stature</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like:</hi> it signifies <hi rend="ital">cut, shape, fashion,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">form:</hi> and more commonly <hi rend="ital">conformation</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proportion:</hi> and hence, <hi rend="ital">beauty,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">justness, of stature;</hi> and simply <hi rend="ital">stature,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">tallness:</hi> pl. <foreign lang="ar">تَقَاطِيعُ</foreign>, which is more commonly used than the sing. in the present day.    </entryFree>2a:T5ae,<entryFree id="n42729" key="تِيَابٌ مُقَطَّعَةٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">تِيَابٌ مُقَطَّعَةٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> [<hi rend="ital">Garments cut out of several pieces</hi>] are <hi rend="ital">such as the shirt, and trousers,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">drawers,</hi> &amp;c. (Mgh in art. <foreign lang="ar">ثوب</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">دَرَاهِمُ مُقَطَّعَةٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Dirhems</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">coins</hi>] <hi rend="ital">that are</hi> [<hi rend="ital">clipped,</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">light of weight,</hi> [or] <hi rend="ital">in which is adulterating alloy:</hi> or, as some say, <hi rend="ital">much broken.</hi> (Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">الحُرُوفُ المُقَطَّعَةُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The letters of the alphabet:</hi> so applied in an explanation of <foreign lang="ar">حُرُوفُ المُعْجَمِ</foreign>, as syn. with this, in the S in art. <foreign lang="ar">عجم</foreign>. See also <foreign lang="ar">حَرْفٌ</foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  See <foreign lang="ar">قِطْعَةٌ</foreign>.
